Statement of Responsibility Laporan Keuangan Konsolidasian Consolidated Financial Statements profil perusahaan coRPORATE profile Didirikan tahun 1962 dan tercatat di Bursa Efek Indonesia Established in 1962 and listed on the Indonesia Stock sejak tahun 1992, PT Sinar Mas Agro Resources and Exchange in 1992, PT Sinar Mas Agro Resources and Technology Tbk (“SMART” atau “Perseroan”) adalah salah satu Technology Tbk (“SMART” or the “Company”) is one of the perusahaan publik produk konsumen berbasis kelapa sawit leading, publicly-listed, integrated palm-based consumer yang terintegrasi dan terkemuka di Indonesia, dengan nilai companies in Indonesia, with total net sales of Rp 29.8 penjualan bersih sebesar Rp 29,8 triliun dan laba sebelum trillion and earnings before interests, taxes, depreciation and beban bunga, pajak, penyusutan dan amortisasi, serta laba amortisation, as well as gain on foreign exchange (EBITDA) selisih kurs (EBITDA) sebesar Rp 2,3 triliun pada tahun 2016. of Rp 2.3 trillion in 2016. Aktivitas utama Perseroan dimulai dari penanaman dan The Company’s primary activities range from cultivating pemanenan pohon kelapa sawit, pengolahan tandan buah and harvesting oil palm trees, processing fresh fruit bunches segar (“TBS”) menjadi minyak sawit (“CPO”) dan inti sawit (“FFB”) into crude palm oil (“CPO”) and palm kernel (“PK”), to (“PK”), pemrosesan CPO menjadi produk industri dan refining CPO into industrial and consumer products such as konsumen seperti minyak goreng, margarin, shortening dan cooking oil, margarine, shortening and biodiesel, as well as biodiesel, serta perdagangan produk berbasis kelapa sawit merchandising palm products throughout the world. ke seluruh dunia. SMART berfokus pada produksi minyak sawit yang lestari. SMART is focused on sustainable palm oil production. The Perseroan mengelola kebun kelapa sawit di Indonesia seluas Company cultivates almost 139,000 hectares of oil palm hampir 139.000 hektar, termasuk lahan plasma. 16 pabrik plantations in Indonesia, including plasma smallholders. Our kelapa sawit kami memproses TBS menjadi CPO dan PK, 16 mills extract CPO and PK from FFB, with a total capacity dengan total kapasitas sebesar 4,2 juta ton per tahun. of 4.2 million tonnes per annum. CPO diproses lebih lanjut menjadi produk bernilai tambah, Our CPO is processed further into value-added bulk, baik curah, industri maupun bermerek, melalui pabrik industrial and branded products through our own refineries, rafinasi kami dengan kapasitas 2,9 juta ton per tahun. PK juga with a total capacity of 2.9 million tonnes per annum. The diproses lebih lanjut di pabrik pengolahan inti sawit dengan PK is crushed in our kernel crushing plants, which have an kapasitas 480 ribu ton per tahun, memproduksi minyak inti annual capacity of 480 thousand tonnes, producing highersawit dan bungkil inti sawit yang bernilai tinggi. value palm kernel oil and palm kernel meal. SMART juga memasarkan dan mengekspor produk SMART also markets and exports palm-based consumer konsumen berbasis kelapa sawit. Selain minyak curah dan products. Besides bulk and industrial oil, SMART’s refined minyak industri, produk turunan SMART juga dipasarkan products are also marketed under several brands, such as dengan berbagai merek, seperti Filma dan Kunci Mas. Saat Filma and Kunci Mas. Today, these brands are recognised for ini, merek-merek tersebut diakui kualitasnya dan memiliki their high quality and command significant market share in pangsa pasar yang signifikan di segmennya masing-masing their respective segments in Indonesia. di Indonesia. Teddy Pawitra Franky Oesman Widjaja Franky Oesman Widjaja Komisaris Utama President Commissioner Bapak Franky Oesman Widjaja, 59 tahun, Warga Negara Mr. Franky Oesman Widjaja, aged 59, an Indonesian citizen, Indonesia, diangkat sebagai Komisaris Utama berdasarkan was appointed as the President Commissioner at the Rapat Umum Pemegang Saham Tahunan (”RUPST”) Annual General Meeting of Shareholders (“AGM”) of the Perseroan tanggal 9 Juni 2015. Beliau juga menjabat Company on 9 June 2015. He also serves as Nominating sebagai anggota Komite Nominasi dan Remunerasi and Remuneration Committee member of the Company, as Perseroan, serta Komisaris Utama PT Dian Swastatika well as the President Commissioner of PT Dian Swastatika Sentosa Tbk dan PT Plaza Indonesia Realty Tbk. Sentosa Tbk and PT Plaza Indonesia Realty Tbk. Beliau terlibat aktif dalam berbagai organisasi, dan saat ini He is active in several organisations. Currently, he menjabat sebagai Co-Chairman Partnership for Indonesia sits as the Co-Chairman of Partnership for Indonesia Sustainable Agriculture (”PISAgro”); Co-Chair World Sustainable Agriculture (“PISAgro”); Co-Chair of World Economic Forum (“WEF”): Grow Asia, dan anggota WEF: Economic Forum (“WEF”): Grow Asia, and a member of Global Agenda Trustee bidang Ketahanan Pangan dan WEF: Global Agenda Trustee for World Food Security Pertanian Dunia. Selain itu beliau juga menjabat sebagai and Agriculture Sector. Severe El Niño in 2015 led to a 13% decrease in fresh fruit bunch (“FFB”) production in 2016, to 2.67 million tonnes, including from plasma estates. The average FFB yield per hectare was 19.50 tonnes, remaining one of the highest in the industry. The harvested FFB are processed in owned milling facilities, which are strategically located near the plantations, to produce crude palm oil (“CPO”) and palm kernel (“PK”). The Company has 16 mills with a combined installed annual capacity of 4.20 million tonnes. During the year, SMART’s mills produced 627,000 tonnes of CPO and 155,000 tonnes of PK. The palm product output was 15% lower compared to the previous year in line with the decrease in FFB production. In 2016, the oil and kernel extraction rates stood at 21.93% and 5.43%, respectively. 32 P T S IN AR MAS AGR O R ES OUR CES AN D TECHNO LO G Y TBK L AP O RAN TAHUNAN 2016 ANNUAL REP O R T Selama tahun berjalan, PKS SMART memproduksi Well-established Downstream Operations with 627.000 ton CPO dan 155.000 ton PK. ETIKA DAN KEPATUHAN Di SMART, kami berkomitmen untuk mencapai tujuan bisnis dengan menjaga integritas dan kepatuhan hukum, di mana pun kami beroperasi. Kami mematuhi hukum yang berlaku di Indonesia di mana kami berbisnis, termasuk peraturan tentang anti suap dan korupsi. Tidak ada insiden penyuapan dan korupsi yang teridentifikasi selama tahun 2016. Pengkonsolidasian entitas anak dimulai Consolidation of a subsidiary begins when pada saat Grup memperoleh pengendalian the Group obtains control over the atas entitas anak dan berakhir pada saat subsidiary and ceases when the Group Grup kehilangan pengendalian atas entitas loses control of the subsidiary. A market is regarded as pelaporan. Pasar dianggap aktif apabila kuotasi active if quoted prices are readily and regularly harga tersedia sewaktu-waktu dan dapat available from an exchange, dealer or broker, diperoleh secara rutin dari bursa, pedagang efek industry group pricing service, or regulatory atau perantara efek, badan penyedia jasa agency, and those prices represent actual and penentuan harga kelompok industri atau badan regularly occurring market transaction on an pengatur, dan harga tersebut mencerminkan arm’s length basis. Instrumen keuangan seperti ini termasuk dalam hirarki Level 1. Tujuan dan Kebijakan Manajemen Risiko 31. Financial Risk Management Objectives and Keuangan Policies Aktivitas Grup terpengaruh berbagai risiko The Group’s activities are exposed to a variety of keuangan: risiko pasar (termasuk risiko mata financial risks: market risk (including currency uang, risiko suku bunga dan risiko harga), risiko risk, fair value interest rate risk and price risk), kredit dan risiko likuiditas. Program manajemen credit risk and liquidity risk. The Group’s overall risiko Grup secara keseluruhan difokuskan pada risk management programme focuses on the pasar keuangan yang tidak dapat diprediksi dan unpredictability of financial markets and seeks to Grup berusaha untuk meminimalkan dampak minimize potential adverse effects on the Group’s yang berpotensi merugikan kinerja keuangan financial performance. The Group uses derivative Grup. Grup menggunakan instrumen keuangan financial instruments to hedge certain risk derivatif untuk lindung nilai atas eksposur risiko exposures. tertentu. 99 PT SINAR MAS AGRO RESOURCES PT SINAR MAS AGRO RESOURCES AND TECHNOLOGY Tbk DAN ENTITAS ANAK AND TECHNOLOGY Tbk AND ITS SUBSIDIARIES Catatan atas Laporan Keuangan Konsolidasian Notes to Consolidated Financial Statements Untuk Tahun-tahun yang Berakhir For the Years Ended 31 Desember 2016 dan 2015 December 31, 2016 and 2015 (Disajikan dalam Jutaan Rupiah, (Expressed in Millions of Rupiah, Kecuali Dinyatakan Lain) Unless Otherwise Stated) Manajemen risiko merupakan tanggung jawab Risk management is the responsibility of the Direksi. Direksi bertugas menentukan prinsip Board of Directors (BOD). The BOD has the dasar kebijakan manajemen risiko Grup secara responsibility to determine the basic principles of keseluruhan serta kebijakan pada area tertentu the Group’s risk management as well as seperti risiko nilai tukar, risiko suku bunga, risiko principles covering specific areas, such as kredit, penggunaan instrumen keuangan derivatif foreign exchange risk, interest rate risk, credit dan instrumen keuangan non-derivatif dan risk, the use of non-derivative and derivative investasi atas kelebihan likuiditas. financial instruments and the investment of excess liquidity. Risiko Suku Bunga Interest Rate Risk Risiko suku bunga adalah risiko dimana nilai Interest rate risk is the risk that the fair value or wajar atau arus kas kontraktual masa datang dari contractual future cash flows of a financial suatu instrumen keuangan akan terpengaruh instrument will be affected due to changes in akibat perubahan suku bunga pasar. Eksposur market interest rates. The Group’s exposure to Grup yang terpengaruh risiko suku bunga the interest rate risk relates primarily to bank terutama terkait dengan utang bank. loans. Untuk meminimalkan risiko suku bunga, To minimize interest rate risk, management manajemen melakukan penelaahan berbagai conducts assessments of interest rates offered suku bunga yang ditawarkan oleh kreditur untuk by creditors to obtain the most favorable interest mendapatkan suku bunga yang menguntungkan rate before taking any decision to enter into a sebelum mengambil keputusan untuk melakukan new loan agreement. perikatan utang.
